             <a id="dd_start">

             <p>
              <a href="http://www.socialblabla.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/10/aplicaciones.jpg">
               <img alt="Lista de 1000 aplicaciones web 2.0" class="alignleft size-full wp-image-775" height="232" src="http://www.socialblabla.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/10/aplicaciones.jpg" title="aplicaciones" width="217"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               AUDIO 2.0
              </strong>
             </p>
             <ul>
              <li>
               Bebop  Compare music calendar against your iTunes catalogue.
               <a href="http://www.bebopular.com/">
                www.bebopular.com/
               </a>
              </li>
              <li>
               Clickcaster  Record, license, publish &amp; promote your radio show.
               <a href="http://www.clickcaster.com/">
                www.clickcaster.com/
               </a>
              </li>
              <li>
               Difm  Radio community.
               <a href="http://www.di.fm/">
                www.di.fm/
               </a>
              </li>
              <li>
               Dottunes  Share your iTunes.
               <a href="http://www.dottunes.net/">
                www.dottunes.net/
               </a>
              </li>
              <li>
               Enablr  Transcribe podcasts, Text2Snailmail, 
               <a href="http://www.enablr.com/">
                www.enablr.com/
               </a>
              </li>
              <li>
               Fluctu8  Create &amp; share your sourcelists.
               <a href="http://fluctu8.com/">
                fluctu8.com/
               </a>
              </li>
              <li>
               Gcast  Podcasting tools &amp; hosting.
               <a href="http://www.gcast.com/">
                www.gcast.com/
               </a>
              </li>
